New commands:

6121 - NoticePatchStart
6122 - NoticePatchData
6123 - NoticePatchFooter
6124 - RequestPatchLineCheck
6125 - RequestPatchFinish

6121 is used after checkversion IF the version is too old -> decrypt version and check
6122 sends the patch in 256 bytes blocks
6124 checks after every 8 blocks, don't know what happens if the check is false !?!
6123 notifies about the end of patch
6125 waits for client to end patch request
